(*******************************************************************************************

 Dependent products in fibrations

 A fibration supports dependent products if every fiber functor `D[{y}] ⟶ D[{x}]` has a
 right adjoint for which the Beck-Chevalley condition is satisfied. In the context of
 first-order logic (i.e., hyperdoctrines), this represents universal quantification, and in
 the context of dependent type theory (i.e., comprehension categories), this represents the
 dependent product operation. In this file, we define the basic notions involving dependent
 products i fibrations and we define when functors preserve dependent products, and we prove
 some basic properties.

 Contents
 1. The Beck-Chevalley condition for right adjoints
 2. Dependent products
 3. Accessors for dependent products
 4. Preservation of dependent products by functors between fibrations
 5. Examples of functors that preserve dependent products

 *******************************************************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

Local Open Scope cat.

(** * 1. The Beck-Chevalley condition for right adjoints *)
Definition right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans
           {C₁ C₂ C₃ C₄ : category}
           {F : C₁ ⟶ C₂}
           {G : C₁ ⟶ C₃}
           {H : C₃ ⟶ C₄}
           {K : C₂ ⟶ C₄}
           (HF : is_left_adjoint F)
           (FR := right_adjoint HF)
           (ε₁ := counit_from_left_adjoint HF)
           (HH : is_left_adjoint H)
           (HR := right_adjoint HH)
           (η₂ := unit_from_left_adjoint HH)
           (τ : nat_z_iso (G ∙ H) (F ∙ K))
  : FR ∙ G ⟹ K ∙ HR
  := nat_trans_comp
       _ _ _
       (pre_whisker (FR ∙ G) η₂)
       (nat_trans_comp
          _ _ _
          (post_whisker (pre_whisker FR τ) HR)
          (post_whisker ε₁ (K ∙ HR))).


C₁, C₂, C₃, C₄: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₁ ⟶ C₃
H: C₃ ⟶ C₄
K: C₂ ⟶ C₄
HF: is_left_adjoint F
FR:= right_adjoint HF: C₂ ⟶ C₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint HF: right_adjoint HF ∙ F ⟹ functor_identity C₂
HH: is_left_adjoint H
HR:= right_adjoint HH: C₄ ⟶ C₃
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint HH: functor_identity C₃ ⟹ H ∙ right_adjoint HH
τ: nat_z_iso (G ∙ H) (F ∙ K)
x: C₂
right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans HF HH τ x =
η₂ (G (FR x)) · # HR (τ (FR x)) · # HR (# K (ε₁ x))


C₁, C₂, C₃, C₄: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₁ ⟶ C₃
H: C₃ ⟶ C₄
K: C₂ ⟶ C₄
HF: is_left_adjoint F
FR:= right_adjoint HF: C₂ ⟶ C₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint HF: right_adjoint HF ∙ F ⟹ functor_identity C₂
HH: is_left_adjoint H
HR:= right_adjoint HH: C₄ ⟶ C₃
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint HH: functor_identity C₃ ⟹ H ∙ right_adjoint HH
τ: nat_z_iso (G ∙ H) (F ∙ K)
x: C₂
right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans HF HH τ x =
η₂ (G (FR x)) · # HR (τ (FR x)) · # HR (# K (ε₁ x))

  apply assoc.
Qed.

Section DependentProduct.
  Context {C : category}
          {D : disp_cat C}
          (HD : cleaving D).

  (** * 2. Dependent products *)
  Definition dependent_product
             {x y : C}
             (f : x --> y)
    : UU
    := is_left_adjoint
         (fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f).

  Definition comm_nat_z_iso_inv
             {w x y z : C}
             (f : x --> w)
             (g : y --> w)
             (h : z --> y)
             (k : z --> x)
             (p : k · f = h · g)
             (F := fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f : D[{w}] ⟶ D[{x}])
             (G := fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD g : D[{w}] ⟶ D[{y}])
             (H := fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD h : D[{y}] ⟶ D[{z}])
             (K := fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD k : D[{x}] ⟶ D[{z}])
    : nat_z_iso (G ∙ H) (F ∙ K)
    := nat_z_iso_inv (comm_nat_z_iso HD f g h k p).

  
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
F:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{x}]
G:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD g: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{y}]
H:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD h: D[{y}] ⟶ D[{z}]
K:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD k: D[{x}] ⟶ D[{z}]
φ: D[{w}]
comm_nat_z_iso_inv f g h k p φ =
fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp HD g h φ
· fiber_functor_on_eq HD (! p) φ
· fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_inv HD f k φ

  
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
F:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{x}]
G:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD g: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{y}]
H:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD h: D[{y}] ⟶ D[{z}]
K:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD k: D[{x}] ⟶ D[{z}]
φ: D[{w}]
comm_nat_z_iso_inv f g h k p φ =
fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp HD g h φ
· fiber_functor_on_eq HD (! p) φ
· fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_inv HD f k φ

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
F:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{x}]
G:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD g: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{y}]
H:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD h: D[{y}] ⟶ D[{z}]
K:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD k: D[{x}] ⟶ D[{z}]
φ: D[{w}]
fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp HD g h φ
· inv_from_z_iso
    (idtoiso
       (maponpaths (λ z0 : C ⟦ z, w ⟧, HD w z z0 φ) p))
· fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_inv HD f k φ =
fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp HD g h φ
· idtoiso
    (maponpaths (λ z0 : C ⟦ z, w ⟧, HD w z z0 φ) (! p))
· fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_inv HD f k φ

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
F:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{x}]
G:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD g: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{y}]
H:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD h: D[{y}] ⟶ D[{z}]
K:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD k: D[{x}] ⟶ D[{z}]
φ: D[{w}]
fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp HD g h φ
· inv_from_z_iso
    (idtoiso
       (maponpaths (λ z0 : C ⟦ z, w ⟧, HD w z z0 φ) p)) =
fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp HD g h φ
· idtoiso
    (maponpaths (λ z0 : C ⟦ z, w ⟧, HD w z z0 φ) (! p))

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
F:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{x}]
G:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD g: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{y}]
H:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD h: D[{y}] ⟶ D[{z}]
K:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD k: D[{x}] ⟶ D[{z}]
φ: D[{w}]
inv_from_z_iso
  (idtoiso
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : C ⟦ z, w ⟧, HD w z z0 φ) p)) =
idtoiso
  (maponpaths (λ z0 : C ⟦ z, w ⟧, HD w z z0 φ) (! p))

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
F:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{x}]
G:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD g: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{y}]
H:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD h: D[{y}] ⟶ D[{z}]
K:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD k: D[{x}] ⟶ D[{z}]
φ: D[{w}]
inv_from_z_iso
  (idtoiso
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : C ⟦ z, w ⟧, HD w z z0 φ)
        (idpath (k · f)))) =
idtoiso
  (maponpaths (λ z0 : C ⟦ z, w ⟧, HD w z z0 φ)
     (! idpath (k · f)))

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
F:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{x}]
G:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD g: D[{w}] ⟶ D[{y}]
H:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD h: D[{y}] ⟶ D[{z}]
K:= fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD k: D[{x}] ⟶ D[{z}]
φ: D[{w}]
id_disp (HD w z (k · f) φ) =
id_disp (HD w z (k · f) φ)

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

  Definition right_beck_chevalley
             {w x y z : C}
             (f : x --> w)
             (g : y --> w)
             (h : z --> y)
             (k : z --> x)
             (p : k · f = h · g)
             (R₁ : dependent_product f)
             (R₂ : dependent_product h)
    : UU
    := ∏ (a : D[{x}]),
       is_z_isomorphism
         (right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans R₁ R₂ (comm_nat_z_iso_inv f g h k p) a).

  
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
R₁: dependent_product f
R₂: dependent_product h
isaprop (right_beck_chevalley f g h k p R₁ R₂)

  
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
R₁: dependent_product f
R₂: dependent_product h
isaprop (right_beck_chevalley f g h k p R₁ R₂)

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
R₁: dependent_product f
R₂: dependent_product h
t: D[{x}]
isofhlevel 1
  ((λ t : D[{x}],
    is_z_isomorphism
      (right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans R₁ R₂
         (comm_nat_z_iso_inv f g h k p) t)) t)

    apply isaprop_is_z_isomorphism.
  Qed.

  Definition has_dependent_products
    : UU
    := ∑ (R : ∏ (x y : C) (f : x --> y), dependent_product f),
       ∏ (w x y z : C)
         (f : x --> w)
         (g : y --> w)
         (h : z --> y)
         (k : z --> x)
         (p : k · f = h · g)
         (H : isPullback p),
       right_beck_chevalley f g h k p (R _ _ f) (R _ _ h).
End DependentProduct.

Section DependentProductPoset.
  Context {C : category}
          {D : disp_cat C}
          (HD : cleaving D)
          (HD' : locally_propositional D)
          (all : ∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ : C) (s : Γ₁ --> Γ₂), D[{Γ₁}] → D[{Γ₂}])
          (all_e : ∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ : C)
                     (s : Γ₁ --> Γ₂)
                     (φ : D[{Γ₁}]),
                   pr1 (HD _ _ s (all _ _ s φ)) -->[ identity _ ] φ)
          (all_i : ∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ : C)
                     (s : Γ₁ --> Γ₂)
                     (ψ : D[{Γ₁}])
                     (χ : D[{Γ₂}])
                     (p : pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₁ s χ) -->[ identity _ ] ψ),
                   χ -->[ identity _ ] all Γ₁ Γ₂ s ψ)
          (all_sub : ∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ Γ₃ Γ₄ : C)
                       (s₁ : Γ₂ --> Γ₁)
                       (s₂ : Γ₃ --> Γ₁)
                       (s₃ : Γ₄ --> Γ₃)
                       (s₄ : Γ₄ --> Γ₂)
                       (p : s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂)
                       (Hp : isPullback p)
                       (φ : D[{Γ₂}]),
                     all Γ₄ Γ₃ s₃ (pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₄ s₄ φ))
                     -->[ identity Γ₃]
                     pr1 (HD Γ₁ Γ₃ s₂ (all Γ₂ Γ₁ s₁ φ))).

  
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
HD': locally_propositional D
all: ∏ Γ₁ Γ₂ : C, C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧ → D[{Γ₁}] → D[{Γ₂}]
all_e: ∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ : C) (s : C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧)
(φ : D[{Γ₁}]),
pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₁ s (all Γ₁ Γ₂ s φ)) -->[
identity Γ₁] φ
all_i: ∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ : C) (s : C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧) 
(ψ : D[{Γ₁}]) (χ : D[{Γ₂}]),
pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₁ s χ) -->[ identity Γ₁] ψ
→ χ -->[ identity Γ₂] all Γ₁ Γ₂ s ψ
all_sub: ∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ Γ₃ Γ₄ : C) (s₁ : C ⟦ Γ₂, Γ₁ ⟧)
(s₂ : C ⟦ Γ₃, Γ₁ ⟧) (s₃ : C ⟦ Γ₄, Γ₃ ⟧)
(s₄ : C ⟦ Γ₄, Γ₂ ⟧) (p : s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂),
isPullback p
→ ∏ φ : D[{Γ₂}],
  all Γ₄ Γ₃ s₃ (pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₄ s₄ φ)) -->[
  identity Γ₃] pr1
                 (HD Γ₁ Γ₃ s₂
                    (all Γ₂ Γ₁ s₁ φ))
Γ₁, Γ₂: C
s: C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧
dependent_product HD s

a ⟧

  identity Γ₃] pr1
                 (HD Γ₁ Γ₃ s₂
                    (all Γ₂ Γ₁ s₁ φ))
Γ₁, Γ₂: C
s: C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧
∏ a : D[{Γ₁}],
is_universal_arrow_from
  (fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD s) a 
  (?G0 a) (?eps a)

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
HD': locally_propositional D
all: ∏ Γ₁ Γ₂ : C, C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧ → D[{Γ₁}] → D[{Γ₂}]
all_e: ∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ : C) (s : C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧)
(φ : D[{Γ₁}]),
pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₁ s (all Γ₁ Γ₂ s φ)) -->[
identity Γ₁] φ
all_i: ∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ : C) (s : C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧) 
(ψ : D[{Γ₁}]) (χ : D[{Γ₂}]),
pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₁ s χ) -->[ identity Γ₁] ψ
→ χ -->[ identity Γ₂] all Γ₁ Γ₂ s ψ
all_sub: ∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ Γ₃ Γ₄ : C) (s₁ : C ⟦ Γ₂, Γ₁ ⟧)
(s₂ : C ⟦ Γ₃, Γ₁ ⟧) (s₃ : C ⟦ Γ₄, Γ₃ ⟧)
(s₄ : C ⟦ Γ₄, Γ₂ ⟧) (p : s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂),
isPullback p
→ ∏ φ : D[{Γ₂}],
  all Γ₄ Γ₃ s₃ (pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₄ s₄ φ)) -->[
  identity Γ₃] pr1
                 (HD Γ₁ Γ₃ s₂
                    (all Γ₂ Γ₁ s₁ φ))
Γ₁, Γ₂: C
s: C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧
D[{Γ₁}] → D[{Γ₂}]
 exact (all _ _ s).

all_sub: ∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ Γ₃ Γ₄ : C) (s₁ : C ⟦ Γ₂, Γ₁ ⟧)
(s₂ : C ⟦ Γ₃, Γ₁ ⟧) (s₃ : C ⟦ Γ₄, Γ₃ ⟧)
(s₄ : C ⟦ Γ₄, Γ₂ ⟧) (p : s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂),
isPullback p
→ ∏ φ : D[{Γ₂}],
  all Γ₄ Γ₃ s₃ (pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₄ s₄ φ)) -->[
  identity Γ₃] pr1
                 (HD Γ₁ Γ₃ s₂
                    (all Γ₂ Γ₁ s₁ φ))
∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧), dependent_product HD f

(s₂ : C ⟦ Γ₃, Γ₁ ⟧) (s₃ : C ⟦ Γ₄, Γ₃ ⟧)

  identity Γ₃] pr1

                    (all Γ₂ Γ₁ s₁ φ))
(λ R : ∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
       dependent_product HD f,
 ∏ (w x y z : C) (f : C ⟦ x, w ⟧) (g : C ⟦ y, w ⟧)
 (h : C ⟦ z, y ⟧) (k : C ⟦ z, x ⟧)
 (p : k · f = h · g),
 isPullback p
 → right_beck_chevalley HD f g h k p (R x w f)
     (R z y h))
  (λ (x y : C) (s : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
   make_dependent_product_of_mor_poset s)
 abstract
        (intros Γ₁ Γ₂ Γ₃ Γ₄ s₁ s₂ s₃ s₄ p Hp φ ;
         simple refine (_ ,, _ ,, _) ; [ | apply HD' | apply HD' ] ;
         exact (all_sub _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ Hp φ)).
  Defined.
End DependentProductPoset.

(** * 3. Accessors for dependent products *)
Section DependentProduct.
  Context {C : category}
          {D : disp_cat C}
          {HD : cleaving D}
          (P : has_dependent_products HD)
          {x y : C}
          (f : x --> y).

  Definition dep_prod
             (xx : D[{x}])
    : D[{y}]
    := right_adjoint (pr1 P x y f) xx.

  Definition dep_prod_mor
             {xx₁ xx₂ : D[{x}]}
             (ff : xx₁ --> xx₂)
    : dep_prod xx₁ --> dep_prod xx₂
    := #(right_adjoint (pr1 P x y f)) ff.

  Definition dep_prod_unit
             (yy : D[{y}])
    : yy -->[ identity y ] dep_prod (fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f yy)
    := unit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 P x y f) yy.

  Definition dep_prod_counit
             (xx : D[{x}])
    : fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f (dep_prod xx) -->[ identity x ] xx
    := counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 P x y f) xx.
End DependentProduct.

(** * 4. Preservation of dependent products by functors between fibrations *)
Definition preserves_dependent_products
           {C₁ C₂ : category}
           {D₁ : disp_cat C₁}
           {HD₁ : cleaving D₁}
           {D₂ : disp_cat C₂}
           {HD₂ : cleaving D₂}
           {F : C₁ ⟶ C₂}
           (FF : cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂)
           (R₁ : has_dependent_products HD₁)
           (R₂ : has_dependent_products HD₂)
  : UU
  := ∏ (x y : C₁)
       (f : x --> y)
       (a : D₁[{x}]),
     is_z_isomorphism
       (right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans
          (pr1 R₁ x y f)
          (pr1 R₂ (F x) (F y) (#F f))
          (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF f)
          a).


C₁, C₂: category
D₁: disp_cat C₁
HD₁: cleaving D₁
D₂: disp_cat C₂
HD₂: cleaving D₂
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
FF: cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂
R₁: has_dependent_products HD₁
R₂: has_dependent_products HD₂
isaprop (preserves_dependent_products FF R₁ R₂)


C₁, C₂: category
D₁: disp_cat C₁
HD₁: cleaving D₁
D₂: disp_cat C₂
HD₂: cleaving D₂
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
FF: cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂
R₁: has_dependent_products HD₁
R₂: has_dependent_products HD₂
isaprop (preserves_dependent_products FF R₁ R₂)

  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: disp_cat C₁
HD₁: cleaving D₁
D₂: disp_cat C₂
HD₂: cleaving D₂
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
FF: cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂
R₁: has_dependent_products HD₁
R₂: has_dependent_products HD₂
t, t0: C₁
t1: C₁ ⟦ t, t0 ⟧
t2: D₁[{t}]
isofhlevel 1
  ((λ t2 : D₁[{t}],
    is_z_isomorphism
      (right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans (pr1 R₁ t t0 t1)
         (pr1 R₂ (F t) (F t0) (# F t1))
         (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
            t1) t2)) t2)

  apply isaprop_is_z_isomorphism.
Qed.

(** * 5. Examples of functors that preserve dependent products *)
Section IdPreserves.
  Context {C : category}
          {D : disp_cat C}
          {HD : cleaving D}
          {x y : C}
          (f : x --> y)
          (P : dependent_product HD f)
          (a : D[{x}]).

  Let R : D[{x}] ⟶ D[{y}]
    := right_adjoint P.
  Let η : functor_identity D[{y}] ⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f ∙ R
    := unit_from_left_adjoint P.
  Let ε : R ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f ⟹ functor_identity _
    := counit_from_left_adjoint P.

  
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
P: dependent_product HD f
a: D[{x}]
R:= right_adjoint P: D[{x}] ⟶ D[{y}]
η:= unit_from_left_adjoint P: functor_identity D[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f ∙ R
ε:= counit_from_left_adjoint P: R ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f
⟹ functor_identity D[{x}]
right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans P P
  (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD HD
     (id_cartesian_disp_functor D) f) a =
η (R a)
· # R
    (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD HD
       (id_cartesian_disp_functor D) f (R a))
· # R (ε a)

· # R
    (identity
       ((fiber_functor (id_cartesian_disp_functor D) y
         ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD
             (# (functor_identity C) f)) (R a)))
· # R (ε a) =
identity
  ((right_adjoint P
    ∙ fiber_functor (id_cartesian_disp_functor D) y) a)

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
P: dependent_product HD f
a: D[{x}]
R:= right_adjoint P: D[{x}] ⟶ D[{y}]
η:= unit_from_left_adjoint P: functor_identity D[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f ∙ R
ε:= counit_from_left_adjoint P: R ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f
⟹ functor_identity D[{x}]
η (R a)
· identity
    (R
       ((fiber_functor (id_cartesian_disp_functor D) y
         ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD
             (# (functor_identity C) f)) (R a)))
· # R (ε a) =
identity
  ((right_adjoint P
    ∙ fiber_functor (id_cartesian_disp_functor D) y) a)

    
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
P: dependent_product HD f
a: D[{x}]
R:= right_adjoint P: D[{x}] ⟶ D[{y}]
η:= unit_from_left_adjoint P: functor_identity D[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f ∙ R
ε:= counit_from_left_adjoint P: R ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f
⟹ functor_identity D[{x}]
η (R a) · # R (ε a) =
identity
  ((right_adjoint P
    ∙ fiber_functor (id_cartesian_disp_functor D) y) a)

    exact (pr222 P a).
  Qed.
End IdPreserves.


C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
P: has_dependent_products HD
preserves_dependent_products
  (id_cartesian_disp_functor D) P P


C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
P: has_dependent_products HD
preserves_dependent_products
  (id_cartesian_disp_functor D) P P

  
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
P: has_dependent_products HD
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: D[{x}]
is_z_isomorphism
  (right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans (pr1 P x y f)
     (pr1 P (functor_identity C x)
        (functor_identity C y)
        (# (functor_identity C) f))
     (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD HD
        (id_cartesian_disp_functor D) f) a)

  
C: category
D: disp_cat C
HD: cleaving D
P: has_dependent_products HD
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: D[{x}]
is_z_isomorphism
  (identity
     ((right_adjoint (pr1 P x y f)
       ∙ fiber_functor (id_cartesian_disp_functor D) y)
        a))

  apply is_z_isomorphism_identity.
Qed.

Section CompPreserves.
  Context {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
          {D₁ : disp_cat C₁}
          {HD₁ : cleaving D₁}
          {D₂ : disp_cat C₂}
          {HD₂ : cleaving D₂}
          {D₃ : disp_cat C₃}
          {HD₃ : cleaving D₃}
          {F : C₁ ⟶ C₂}
          {G : C₂ ⟶ C₃}
          (FF : cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂)
          (GG : cartesian_disp_functor G D₂ D₃)
          {x y : C₁}
          (f : x --> y)
          (a : D₁[{x}])
          (P₁ : dependent_product HD₁ f)
          (P₂ : dependent_product HD₂ (#F f))
          (P₃ : dependent_product HD₃ (#G (#F f))).

  Let R₁ : D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
    := right_adjoint P₁.
  Let η₁ : functor_identity _ ⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
    := unit_from_left_adjoint P₁.
  Let ε₁ : R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ⟹ functor_identity _
    := counit_from_left_adjoint P₁.

  Let R₂ : D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
    := right_adjoint P₂.
  Let η₂ : functor_identity _ ⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (#F f) ∙ R₂
    := unit_from_left_adjoint P₂.
  Let ε₂ : R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (#F f) ⟹ functor_identity _
    := counit_from_left_adjoint P₂.

  Let R₃ : D₃[{G(F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G(F y)}]
    := right_adjoint P₃.
  Let η₃ : functor_identity _ ⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃ (#G(#F f)) ∙ R₃
    := unit_from_left_adjoint P₃.
  Let ε₃ : R₃ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃ (#G(#F f)) ⟹ functor_identity _
    := counit_from_left_adjoint P₃.

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: disp_cat C₁
HD₁: cleaving D₁
D₂: disp_cat C₂
HD₂: cleaving D₂
D₃: disp_cat C₃
HD₃: cleaving D₃

GG: cartesian_disp_functor G D₂ D₃
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: D₁[{x}]
P₁: dependent_product HD₁ f
P₂: dependent_product HD₂ (# F f)
P₃: dependent_product HD₃ (# G (# F f))
R₁:= right_adjoint P₁: D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₁: functor_identity D₁[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans P₁ P₃
  (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₃
     (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG) f) a =
η₃
  (fiber_functor (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG) y
     (R₁ a))
· # R₃
    (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₃
       (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG) f (R₁ a))
· # R₃
    (# (fiber_functor
          (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG) x)
       (ε₁ a))

  Let φ
    := #(fiber_functor GG (F y))
          (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
           · # R₂ (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF f (R₁ a))
           · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))).

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: disp_cat C₁
HD₁: cleaving D₁
D₂: disp_cat C₂
HD₂: cleaving D₂
D₃: disp_cat C₃
HD₃: cleaving D₃
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₂ ⟶ C₃
FF: cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂
GG: cartesian_disp_functor G D₂ D₃
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: D₁[{x}]
P₁: dependent_product HD₁ f
P₂: dependent_product HD₂ (# F f)
P₃: dependent_product HD₃ (# G (# F f))
R₁:= right_adjoint P₁: D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₁: functor_identity D₁[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
φ
· η₃
    (pr1 GG (F y)
       (R₂
          (fiber_functor FF x
             (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a)))) =
η₃
  (fiber_functor GG (F y)
     (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
        (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))))
· # R₃
    (# (fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
          (# G (# F f))) φ)

F: C₁ ⟶ C₂

x, y: C₁

a: D₁[{x}]
P₁: dependent_product HD₁ f
P₂: dependent_product HD₂ (# F f)
P₃: dependent_product HD₃ (# G (# F f))
R₁:= right_adjoint P₁: D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₁: functor_identity D₁[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
φ
· η₃
    (pr1 GG (F y)
       (R₂
          (fiber_functor FF x
             (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a)))) =
η₃
  (fiber_functor GG (F y)
     (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
        (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))))
· # R₃
    (# (fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
          (# G (# F f))) φ)

    apply (nat_trans_ax η₃).
  Qed.

     (fiber_functor FF x

  (disp_functor_composite_is_cartesian_disp_functor
     (cartesian_disp_functor_is_cartesian FF)
     (cartesian_disp_functor_is_cartesian GG) y x f
     (R₁ a) (HD₁ y x f (R₁ a)) (HD₁ y x f (R₁ a))
     (HD₁ y x f (R₁ a))) (identity (G (F x)))
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₃ ⟦ G (F x), G (F y) ⟧,
      HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x)) (# G (# F f))
        (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))) -->[
      z] GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a)))
     (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)
     (HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x)) (# G (# F f))
        (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))))) =
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x)) (# G (# F f))
        (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))))
     (GG (F x) (FF x (HD₁ y x f (R₁ a)))))
  (id_right (identity (G (F x))))
  (cartesian_factorisation
     (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian GG
        (HD₂ (F y) (F x) ((# F)%cat f) (FF y (R₁ a))))
     (identity (G (F x)))

        (λ z : C₃ ⟦ G (F x), G (F y) ⟧,

           ((# G)%cat ((# F)%cat f))

         z] GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a)))
        (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof
           ((# F)%cat f))
        (HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x))
           ((# G)%cat ((# F)%cat f))
           (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))))) ;; transportf
                                           (mor_disp

                                                 (FF y

            (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))) -->[
          z] GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a)))
         (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof
            ((# F)%cat f))
         (HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x))
            ((# G)%cat ((# F)%cat f))
            (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))))) ;; transportf

C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: disp_cat C₁

F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₂ ⟶ C₃

a: D₁[{x}]
P₁: dependent_product HD₁ f

R₁:= right_adjoint P₁: D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₁: functor_identity D₁[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))

φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
(transportf
   (mor_disp
      (HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x))
         ((# G)%cat ((# F)%cat f))
         (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))))
      (GG (F x) (FF x (HD₁ y x f (R₁ a)))))
   (id_right (identity (G (F x))))
   (cartesian_factorisation
      (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian GG
         (HD₂ (F y) (F x) ((# F)%cat f) (FF y (R₁ a))))
      (identity (G (F x)))
      (transportf
         (λ z : C₃ ⟦ G (F x), G (F y) ⟧,
          HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x))
            ((# G)%cat ((# F)%cat f))
            (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))) -->[
          z] GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a)))
         (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof
            ((# F)%cat f))
         (HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x))
            ((# G)%cat ((# F)%cat f))
            (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))))) ;; transportf
                                            (mor_disp
                                               (GG
                                                 (F x)

                                                 (F y)

                                                 z]

               ((# G)%cat ((# F)%cat f))
               (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))) -->[
             z] GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a)))
            (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof
               ((# F)%cat f))
            (HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x))
               ((# G)%cat ((# F)%cat f))
               (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))))) ;; ♯ GG
                                               (cartesian_factorisation
                                                 (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian
                                                 FF
                                                 (HD₁
                                                 y x f
                                                 (R₁ a)))

                                                 (F x))

                                                 (F y)

                                                 z]

                                                 f)
                                                 (HD₂
                                                 (F y)
                                                 (F x)
                                                 ((# F)%cat
                                                 f)
                                                 (FF y
                                                 (R₁ a))))))) ;; 
 ♯ (disp_functor_composite FF GG) (HD₁ y x f (R₁ a)))%mor_disp =

     (identity (G (F x)) · identity (G (F x)))

       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF

D₁: disp_cat C₁
HD₁: cleaving D₁
D₂: disp_cat C₂
HD₂: cleaving D₂
D₃: disp_cat C₃
HD₃: cleaving D₃
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₂ ⟶ C₃
FF: cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂
GG: cartesian_disp_functor G D₂ D₃
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: D₁[{x}]
P₁: dependent_product HD₁ f
P₂: dependent_product HD₂ (# F f)
P₃: dependent_product HD₃ (# G (# F f))
R₁:= right_adjoint P₁: D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₁: functor_identity D₁[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x)) (# G (# F f))
        (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))))
     (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))))
  (maponpaths (compose (identity (G (F x))))
     (maponpaths # G
        (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)) @
   maponpaths (compose (identity (G (F x))))
     (functor_comp G (identity (F x)) (# F f)) @
   assoc (identity (G (F x))) (# G (identity (F x)))
     (# G (# F f)) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity (G (F x)) · # G (identity (F x)))
     (identity (G (F x)) · identity (G (F x)))
     (# G (# F f))
     (maponpaths (compose (identity (G (F x))))
        (functor_id G (F x))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity (G (F x)) · identity (G (F x)))
     (identity (G (F x))) (# G (# F f))
     (id_right (identity (G (F x)))))
  (cartesian_factorisation
     (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian GG
        (HD₂ (F y) (F x) ((# F)%cat f) (FF y (R₁ a))))
     (identity (G (F x)))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₃ ⟦ G (F x), G (F y) ⟧,
         HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x))
           ((# G)%cat ((# F)%cat f))
           (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))) -->[
         z] GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a)))
        (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof
           ((# F)%cat f))
        (HD₃ (G (F y)) (G (F x))
           ((# G)%cat ((# F)%cat f))
           (GG (F y) (FF y (R₁ a))))) ;; ♯ GG
                                           (HD₂ (F y)
                                              (F x)
                                              ((# F)%cat
                                                 f)
                                              (FF y
                                                 (R₁ a))))%mor_disp =
?b

  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans P₁ P₃
  (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₃
     (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG) f) a =
# (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans P₁ P₂
     (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF f) a)
· right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans P₂ P₃
    (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₂ HD₃ GG
       (# F f)) (FF x a)

P₂: dependent_product HD₂ (# F f)
P₃: dependent_product HD₃ (# G (# F f))
R₁:= right_adjoint P₁: D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₁: functor_identity D₁[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans P₁ P₃
  (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₃
     (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG) f) a =
# (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans P₁ P₂
     (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF f) a)
· right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans P₂ P₃
    (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₂ HD₃ GG
       (# F f)) (FF x a)

ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
# (fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃ (# G (# F f)))
  (# (fiber_functor GG (F y))

      · # R₂

· (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₂ HD₃ GG (# F f)
     (R₂ (FF x a))
   · # (fiber_functor GG (F x)) (ε₂ (FF x a))) = ?b

D₃: disp_cat C₃
HD₃: cleaving D₃
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₂ ⟶ C₃
FF: cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂
GG: cartesian_disp_functor G D₂ D₃
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: D₁[{x}]
P₁: dependent_product HD₁ f
P₂: dependent_product HD₂ (# F f)
P₃: dependent_product HD₃ (# G (# F f))
R₁:= right_adjoint P₁: D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₁: functor_identity D₁[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
?b =
fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₃
  (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG) f (R₁ a)
· # (fiber_functor (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG)
       x) (ε₁ a)

P₂: dependent_product HD₂ (# F f)
P₃: dependent_product HD₃ (# G (# F f))
R₁:= right_adjoint P₁: D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₁: functor_identity D₁[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧

ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
fiber_functor_natural HD₂ HD₃ GG (# F f)
  (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
     (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a)))
· # (fiber_functor GG (F x))
    (# (functor_identity D₂[{F x}])
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF f
          (R₁ a) · # (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))) =
fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₃
  (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG) f (R₁ a)
· # (fiber_functor (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG)
       x) (ε₁ a)

G: C₂ ⟶ C₃
FF: cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂
GG: cartesian_disp_functor G D₂ D₃
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: D₁[{x}]
P₁: dependent_product HD₁ f
P₂: dependent_product HD₂ (# F f)
P₃: dependent_product HD₃ (# G (# F f))
R₁:= right_adjoint P₁: D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₁: functor_identity D₁[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₃
  (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG) f (R₁ a)
· # (fiber_functor (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG)
       x) (ε₁ a) = ?b

G: C₂ ⟶ C₃
FF: cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂
GG: cartesian_disp_functor G D₂ D₃
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: D₁[{x}]
P₁: dependent_product HD₁ f
P₂: dependent_product HD₂ (# F f)
P₃: dependent_product HD₃ (# G (# F f))
R₁:= right_adjoint P₁: D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₁: functor_identity D₁[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
transportf
  (mor_disp (GG (F x) (FF x (HD₁ y x f (R₁ a))))
     (GG (F x) (FF x a)))
  (maponpaths # G (functor_id F x) @
   functor_id G (F x)) ((♯ GG)%mor_disp (♯ FF (ε₁ a))) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (GG (F x) (FF x (HD₁ y x f (R₁ a))))
     (GG (F x) (FF x a))) (functor_id G (F x))
  ((♯ GG)%mor_disp
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (FF x (HD₁ y x f (R₁ a))) (FF x a))
        (functor_id F x) ((♯ FF)%mor_disp (ε₁ a))))

     (GG (F x) (FF x a))) (functor_id G (F x))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (GG (F x) (FF x (HD₁ y x f (R₁ a))))
        (GG (F x) (FF x a)))
     (maponpaths # G (functor_id F x))
     ((♯ GG)%mor_disp (♯ FF (ε₁ a))))

C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: disp_cat C₁
HD₁: cleaving D₁
D₂: disp_cat C₂
HD₂: cleaving D₂
D₃: disp_cat C₃
HD₃: cleaving D₃
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₂ ⟶ C₃
FF: cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂
GG: cartesian_disp_functor G D₂ D₃
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: D₁[{x}]
P₁: dependent_product HD₁ f
P₂: dependent_product HD₂ (# F f)
P₃: dependent_product HD₃ (# G (# F f))
R₁:= right_adjoint P₁: D₁[{x}] ⟶ D₁[{y}]
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₁: functor_identity D₁[{y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f ∙ R₁
ε₁:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₁: R₁ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₁ HD₁ f
⟹ functor_identity D₁[{x}]
R₂:= right_adjoint P₂: D₂[{F x}] ⟶ D₂[{F y}]
η₂:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₂: functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f) ∙ R₂
ε₂:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₂: R₂ ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₂ HD₂ (# F f)
⟹ functor_identity D₂[{F x}]
R₃:= right_adjoint P₃: D₃[{G (F x)}] ⟶ D₃[{G (F y)}]
η₃:= unit_from_left_adjoint P₃: functor_identity D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟹ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f)) ∙ R₃
ε₃:= counit_from_left_adjoint P₃: R₃
∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving D₃ HD₃
    (# G (# F f))
⟹ functor_identity D₃[{G (F x)}]
φ:= # (fiber_functor GG (F y))
  (η₂ (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))
   · # R₂
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF
          f (R₁ a))
   · # R₂ (# (fiber_functor FF x) (ε₁ a))): D₃[{G (F y)}]
⟦ fiber_functor GG (F y)
    (functor_identity D₂[{F y}]
       (fiber_functor FF y (R₁ a))),
fiber_functor GG (F y)
  (R₂
     (fiber_functor FF x
        (functor_identity D₁[{x}] a))) ⟧
maponpaths # G (functor_id F x) @ functor_id G (F x) =
maponpaths # G (functor_id F x) @ functor_id G (F x)

    apply homset_property.
  Qed.
End CompPreserves.

F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₂ ⟶ C₃
FF: cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂
GG: cartesian_disp_functor G D₂ D₃
P₁: has_dependent_products HD₁
P₂: has_dependent_products HD₂
P₃: has_dependent_products HD₃
HFF: preserves_dependent_products FF P₁ P₂
HGG: preserves_dependent_products GG P₂ P₃
preserves_dependent_products
  (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG) P₁ P₃

D₁: disp_cat C₁
HD₁: cleaving D₁
D₂: disp_cat C₂
HD₂: cleaving D₂
D₃: disp_cat C₃
HD₃: cleaving D₃
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G: C₂ ⟶ C₃
FF: cartesian_disp_functor F D₁ D₂
GG: cartesian_disp_functor G D₂ D₃
P₁: has_dependent_products HD₁

P₃: has_dependent_products HD₃

HGG: preserves_dependent_products GG P₂ P₃
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
a: D₁[{x}]
is_z_isomorphism
  (right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans (pr1 P₁ x y f)
     (pr1 P₃ ((F ∙ G) x) ((F ∙ G) y) (# (F ∙ G) f))
     (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₃
        (comp_cartesian_disp_functor FF GG) f) a)

a: D₁[{x}]
is_z_isomorphism
  (# (fiber_functor GG (F y))
     (right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans (pr1 P₁ x y f)
        (pr1 P₂ (F x) (F y) (# F f))
        (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₁ HD₂ FF f)
        a)
   · right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans
       (pr1 P₂ (F x) (F y) (# F f))
       (pr1 P₃ (G (F x)) (G (F y)) (# G (# F f)))
       (fiber_functor_natural_nat_z_iso HD₂ HD₃ GG
          (# F f)) (FF x a))
